        <!--Content section--> 
        <div id="ctl00_ctl00_div_content_sec" class="div_content_sec"> 
         <a id="content"></a> 
         <noscript> 
          <div style="width:800px;background-color:#ffffff;FONT-WEIGHT:bold;FONT-SIZE:12pt;COLOR:red">
           <br /> It appears that your browser does not support JavaScript, or you have it disabled. This site is best viewed with JavaScript enabled. If JavaScript or cookies are disabled in your browser, please enable them and then reload this page.&nbsp;

         <div id="ctl00_ctl00_Content_ctl00_dvHtmlContent" style="text-align :left; min-width :200 px">
          <script type="text/javascript">

/***********************************************
* MultiFrame Image Slideshow script- &#169; Dynamic Drive DHTML code library (www.dynamicdrive.com)
* This notice MUST stay intact for legal use
* Visit Dynamic Drive at http://www.dynamicdrive.com/ for full source code
***********************************************/

var seqslides=new Array()
//Set Path to Image plus optional URL ("" for no URL):
seqslides[0]=["http://www.ucrcampusstore.ucr.edu/SiteImages/115-SchoolImages/115-New%20Images/115-TW_2014.png", "http://www.ucrcampusstore.ucr.edu/MerchList.aspx?id=14732", "Tartan Wear available at UCR Campus Store"]
seqslides[1]=["http://www.ucrcampusstore.ucr.edu/SiteImages/115-SchoolImages/115-New%20Images/115-PSGP_2014.png", "", "Pride Sash preview event, March 12, 10am-2pm, HUB lounge inside UCR Campus Store"]
seqslides[2]=["http://www.ucrcampusstore.ucr.edu/SiteImages/115-SchoolImages/115-New%20Images/115-ipadmini.png", "", "Apple iPad mini now available at UCR Campus Store"]

//Set pause between each image display (8000=8 second):
var slidedelay=8000

//Set how many images to show at once (must be less than total # of images above):
var slidestoreveal=1

//Specify code to insert between each slide (ie: "<br>" to insert a line break and create a vertical layout)
//"" for none (or horizontal):
var slideseparater="<br>"

//Set optional link target to be added to all images with a link:
var optlinktarget="secwindow"

//Set image border width:
var imgborderwidth=0

//Set opacity value of each image when it's "dimmed", and when it's not, respectively (1=100% opaque/normal).
//Change 0.2 to 0 to completely hide image when it's dimmed:
var opacityvalues=[0.2,1]

///No need to edit beyond here///////////

function processimgcode(theimg){
var imghtml=""
if (theimg[1]!="")
imghtml='<a href="'+theimg[1]+'" target="'+optlinktarget+'">'
imghtml+='<img src="'+theimg[0]+'" border="'+imgborderwidth+'" style="filter:alpha(opacity='+(opacityvalues[0]*100)+');-moz-opacity:'+opacityvalues[0]+'" alt="'+theimg[2]+'">'
if (theimg[1]!="")
imghtml+='</a>'
return imghtml
}

var curslide=1 //var to track current slide (total: slidestoreveal)
var curimgindex=0 //var to track current image (total: seqslides.length)
var isfirstcycle=1 //boolean to indicate whether this is the first cycle

if (document.getElementById){
for (i=0;i<slidestoreveal;i++)
document.write('<span id="seqslide'+i+'" class="seqslidestyle">'+processimgcode(seqslides[i])+'</span>'+slideseparater)
curimgindex=slidestoreveal
illuminateslide(0,opacityvalues[1])
}

function illuminateslide(slideindex, amt){
var slideobj=document.getElementById("seqslide"+slideindex).getElementsByTagName("IMG")[0]
if (slideobj.filters)
slideobj.filters.alpha.opacity=amt*100
else if (slideobj.style.MozOpacity)
slideobj.style.MozOpacity=amt
}

function displayit(){
if (curslide<slidestoreveal){
if (!isfirstcycle)
changeimage(curslide)
illuminateslide(curslide, opacityvalues[1])
curslide++
}
else{
isfirstcycle=0
for (i=0;i<slidestoreveal;i++)
illuminateslide(i, opacityvalues[0])
changeimage(0)
illuminateslide(0, opacityvalues[1])
curslide=1
}
}

function changeimage(slideindex){
document.getElementById("seqslide"+slideindex).innerHTML=processimgcode(seqslides[curimgindex])
curimgindex++
if (curimgindex>=seqslides.length)
curimgindex=0
}

if (document.getElementById)
setInterval("displayit()",slidedelay)


</script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
    Sys.WebForms.PageRequestManager.getInstance().add_endRequest(endRequest);
    function endRequest(sender, e) {
        if (e.get_error()) {
            document.getElementById("err").innerText = e.get_error().description;
            e.set_errorHandled(true);
        }
    }
</script>

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").each(function () {

            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").focus(function () {
                $(this).removeClass("GoogleWatermark"); // handle all focus hints
            });

            $("#txtGoogleSearch").blur(function () {
                ToggleHint(this); // handle all blur hints
            });
        });

        function ToggleHint(obj) {
            if ($(obj).val() == '') { $(obj).addClass("GoogleWatermark"); };
        }

      <a href="https://ucribm.ucr.edu/Paws/PAWS.html" target="_blank"> <img id="growlBtn" src="/Images/home/growl_login_btn_default.png" title="" onmouseover="this.src='/Images/home/growl_login_btn_hover.png'" onmouseout="this.src='/Images/home/growl_login_btn_default.png'" alt="Log into GROWL" /> </a> 
      <a href="http://rweb.ucr.edu/" target="_blank"> <img id="Img1" src="/Images/home/RWeb_login_btn_default.png" title="" onmouseover="this.src='/Images/home/RWeb_login_btn_hover.png'" onmouseout="this.src='/Images/home/RWeb_login_btn_default.png'" alt="Log into RWEB" /> </a>

    <div class="span-18 last" style="padding-bottom: 30px;"> 
     <p>When two or more courses are merged into one course, follow the procedures outlined in the following example:</p> 
     <h3>ECON 100A and ECON 100B are renumbered to ECON 100</h3> 
     <ol> 
      <li>Click <strong>Search/Modify</strong> Course at the CRAMS main menu.</li> 
      <li>Search for ECON 100A and select the appropriate (usually the most recent) version of the course.</li> 
      <li>Click Save Work to make a working copy of the course.</li> 
      <li>Modify the course as needed (see the <a href="modify-a-course.aspx">&quot;Modify a Course Guide&quot;</a>, or <a href="cross-listed-courses.aspx">&quot;Dealing with Cross-Listed Courses Guide&quot;</a> for detailed instructions).</li> 
      <li>To change the course from ECON 100A to ECON 100, remove &quot;A&quot; from the Course Suffix field.</li> 
      <li>Before submitting ECON 100, enter the following information in the Renumbered From field:</li> 
      <ul> 
       <li>ECON 100A, ECON 100B</li> 
      </ul> 
      <li>Submit ECON 100.</li> 
      <li><strong>DO NOT</strong> submit a Course Proposal for ECON 100B. Upon approval of ECON 100, the Registrar's Office will discontinue ECON 100B and enter the following information in its Closing Notes field.</li> 
     </ol> 
     <h3>ECON 100A and ECON 100B renumbered to ECON 100<strong><br /> </strong></h3> 
     <p> The department searches for ECON 100A, clicks the Save button to create a working copy, and updates the following fields as illustrated below: </p> 
     <ul style="list-style:disc;"> 
      <li>Course suffix (removes the A)</li> 
      <li>Renumbered From</li> 
      <li>Closing Notes</li> 
      <li>1st Effective Quarter and Year<br /> <br /> <br /> <img style="width: 454px; height: 373px" border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/Chapter14.JPG" width="589" height="485" /><br /> </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p> <br /> <br /> After ECON 100 is approved, the Registrar's Office updates the following field of ECON 100A as illustrated below: </p> 
     <ul style="list-style:disc;"> 
      <li>Closing Notes<br /> <br /> </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p align="center"> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter14two.jpg" /><br /> </p> 
     <p>After ECON 100 is approved, the Registrar's Office updates the following fields of ECON 100B as illustrated below:</p> 
     <ul style="list-style:disc;"> 
      <li>Closing Notes<br /> Last Effective Quarter and Year<br /> <br /> </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p align="center"> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter14three.jpg" /></p> 
     <p> <br /> </p> 
     <p><b>The following example does not involve a merge but is included in these instructions because of its similarity to a merge:</b></p> 
     <h3>CHN 020A is renumbered to CHN 020; CHN 020B is deleted</h3> 
     <ol> 
      <li>Click <b>Search/Modify Course</b> at the CRAMS main menu.</li> 
      <li>Search for CHN 020A and select the appropriate (usually the most recent) version of the course.</li> 
      <li>Click Save Work to make a working copy of the course.</li> 
      <li>Modify the course as needed (see <a href="modify-a-course.aspx">&quot;Modify a Course Guide&quot;</a>, or <a href="cross-listed-courses.aspx">&quot;Dealing with Cross-Listed Courses Guide&quot;</a>, for detailed instructions).</li> 
      <li>To change the course from CHN 020A to CHN 020, remove &quot;A&quot; from the Course Suffix field.</li> 
      <li>Before submitting CHN 020, enter CHN 020A in the Renumbered From field.</li> 
      <li>Submit CHN 020. </li> 
      <li>Click Search/Modify Course at the CRAMS main menu.</li> 
      <li>Search for CHN 020B and select the appropriate (usually the most recent) version of the course.</li> 
      <li>Delete CHN 020B (see <a href="delete-a-course.aspx">&quot;Delete a Course Guide&quot;</a>, for detailed instructions).</li> 
      <li>Submit CHN 020B. </li> 
     </ol> 
     <p>The department searches for CHN020A, clicks the Save button to create a working copy, and updates the following fields as illustrated below:</p> 
     <ul style="list-style:disc;"> 
      <li>Course Suffix (removes the A)</li> 
      <li>Renumbered From</li> 
      <li>1st Effective Quarter and Year<br /> <br /> <br /> </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p align="center"> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter14four.jpg" /><br /> <br /> <br /> <br /> </p> 
     <p> The department searches for CHN 020B, clicks Tools and then Delete Course to create a working copy, and updates the following fields as illustrated below: </p> 
     <ul style="list-style:disc;"> 
      <li>1st effective Quarter and Year<br /> <br /> </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p align="center"> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter14five.jpg" /></p> 
     <p> <br /> <br /> <br /> After CHN 020 and the deletion of CHN 020B are approved, the Registrar's Office updates the following field of CHN 020A as illustrated below: </p> 
     <ul style="list-style:disc;"> 
      <li>Closing Notes<br /> </li> 
     </ul> 
     <p align="center"> <img border="0" alt="" src="../../images/course-mgt/chapter14six.jpg" /><br /> </p> 
    </div>

     <script type="text/javascript" src="http://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jquery/1.7.2/jquery.min.js"></script> 
     <script type="text/javascript" src="http://ajax.googleapis.com/ajax/libs/jqueryui/1.8.18/jquery-ui.min.js"></script>

     <script type="text/javascript" src="/js/plugin/jquery.jcarousel.min.js"></script> 
     <script type="text/javascript">

var calserver = "http://ragsm.ucr.edu/agsmevents/";
var prog      = "mba";
var ishover   = false;
var autorate  = 7;
var animrate  = 'fast';

function scarousel_initCallback(carousel) {
  $('#jd_news_sidebar').hover(function() {
	ishover = true;
    carousel.startAuto(0);
    carousel.animation(0);
  }, function() {
    ishover = false;
    carousel.animation(animrate);
    carousel.startAuto(autorate);
  });

}

$(document).ready(function(){

  var path = document.location.pathname;
  var dir = path.substring(path.indexOf('/', 0)+1, path.lastIndexOf('/'));

  if (dir == "calendar") {
    $("#sidebar_events").hide();
  } else {
    $.getJSON(calserver + "ae_get_website_sidebar.php?jsoncallback=?&prog="+prog,
    function(data) {
      $("#jd_news_sidebar").html(data.sidebar);
      $('#jd_news_sidebar ul').attr('id','sidebar_carousel');
      //$('div.jd_news_scroll').jdNewsScroll();
      $('#sidebar_carousel').jcarousel({
        initCallback: scarousel_initCallback,
        vertical: true,
        scroll: 1,
        auto: autorate,
		wrap: 'last',
		animation: animrate
      });
    });
  }

});

</script>

     <h3>Quality Business Education in Southern California: MBA, Flex MBA, MPAc, MFin</h3> 
     <p><a href="http://soba.ucr.edu/aacsb/" target="_blank"><img class="img_R_borderless" src="/images/seals_agsm.png" alt="Seals" /></a>With a nationally-ranked and internationally-recognized MBA program, the <a href="http://soba.ucr.edu/aacsb/" target="_blank">AACSB-accredited</a> A. Gary Anderson Graduate School of Management (AGSM) at the <a href="http://soba.ucr.edu" target="_blank">UCR School of Business Administration (SoBA)</a>, is one of the fastest growing graduate business schools in Southern California, shaping the future by developing leading thinkers who will stand at the forefront of business growth.&nbsp;</p>

      <!--
Hover <span id="hdata">zzz</span><br />
In/Out <span id="iodata">zzz</span><br />
Slider <span id="sldata">zzz</span><br />
Index <span id="idxdata">zzz</span><br />
--> 
      <script type="text/javascript">
  history.navigationMode = 'compatible';

  var t, st;
  var lastidx;
  var ishover = false;
  var isscrolling = false;
  var tcar;
  var nbritems = 0;
  var idlist  = new Array();
  var vsl = 1;
  var sauto = 8;
  var sshow = 3;

function mycarousel_itemFirstInCallback(carousel, item, idx, state) {
  var idm = ((idx-1) % nbritems) + 1;
  if (idm <= 0) idm = nbritems + idm;
  $('#slider').slider('option', 'value', idm);
  lastidx = idx;
  $("#idxdata").html(lastidx + " (" + idm + ") /" + nbritems);
  return true;
};


function mycarousel_resetAuto() {
  if (ishover) {
    t = setTimeout("mycarousel_resetAuto();", 6000);
  } else {
    tcar.startAuto(sauto);
  }
  return true;
};

function mycarousel_setSlider() {
  clearTimeout(st);
  if (isscrolling) {
	$("#sldata").html("scrolling " + vsl);
    st = setTimeout("mycarousel_setSlider();", 250);
  } else {
	$("#sldata").html("set " + vsl);
    tcar.scroll(parseInt(vsl),false);
  }
  return true;
};

function mycarousel_initCallback(carousel) {
  tcar = carousel;
  if (nbritems > sshow ) {

	$('#slider').bind('slide', function(event,ui) {
		clearTimeout(st);
		clearTimeout(t);
		carousel.startAuto(0);
		vsl = ui.value;
		if (isscrolling) {
		  $("#sldata").html("scrolling " + vsl);
          st = setTimeout("mycarousel_setSlider();", 250);
		} else {
		  mycarousel_setSlider();
		}

		t = setTimeout("mycarousel_resetAuto();", 6000);
    });


    // Disable autoscrolling if the user clicks the prev or next button.
    carousel.buttonNext.bind('click', function() {
		clearTimeout(t);
		t = setTimeout("mycarousel_resetAuto();", 6000);
        carousel.startAuto(0);
    });

    carousel.buttonPrev.bind('click', function() {
		clearTimeout(t);
		t = setTimeout("mycarousel_resetAuto();", 6000);
        carousel.startAuto(0);
    });

    // Pause autoscrolling if the user moves with the cursor over the clip.
    //carousel.clip.hover(function() {
    $('#mycarousel').hover(function() {
        clearTimeout(t);
        ishover = true;
        //carousel.stopAuto();
		carousel.startAuto(0);
		$("#hdata").html("is hover");
    }, function() {
		clearTimeout(t);
		$("#hdata").html("is not hover");
		ishover = false;
        //carousel.startAuto(3);
		t = setTimeout("mycarousel_resetAuto();", 6000);
    });
  } else {
    carousel.startAuto(0);
    $("#slider").hide();
    $("#news_carousel").find(".jcarousel-next").hide();
    $("#news_carousel").find(".jcarousel-prev").hide();
  }
  return true;

};


function mycarousel_itemVisibleInCallback(carousel, item, i, state, evt) {
  // The index() method calculates the index from a
  // given index who is out of the actual item range.
  $("#iodata").html("in " + state);
  if (state != "init") isscrolling = true;
  var idx = carousel.index(i, idlist.length) - 1;
  var izz = idlist[idx];
  carousel.add(i, mycarousel_getItemHTML(izz));
  return true;
};

function mycarousel_itemVisibleOutCallback(carousel, item, i, state, evt) {
    carousel.remove(i);
	isscrolling = false;
	$("#iodata").html("out " + state);
  return true;
};

/**
 * Item html creation helper.
 */
function mycarousel_getItemHTML(item) {
  return '<div "id="newsactive' + item + '" >' + $("#newsid" + item).html() + '</div>';
};

$(document).ready(function() {

  $("#holder").hide();
  $("#slider").slider({ min: 1, max: 1 });

  $.getJSON(newsserver + "an_get_news_list.php?jsoncallback=?",
    function(nwdata) {
      //alert("Count: " + nwdata.nbrarticles);
      nbritems = parseInt(nwdata.nbrarticles);
      idlist   = nwdata.idlist;
      $('#slider').slider('option', 'max', nbritems-(sshow-1));
      $('#mycarousel').jcarousel({
        auto: sauto,
        scroll: 1,
        animation: 1000,
        wrap: 'circular',
        animatebuttons: false,
        initCallback: mycarousel_initCallback,
        itemFirstInCallback: {onBeforeAnimation: mycarousel_itemFirstInCallback},
        itemVisibleInCallback: {onBeforeAnimation: mycarousel_itemVisibleInCallback},
        itemVisibleOutCallback: {onAfterAnimation: mycarousel_itemVisibleOutCallback}
      });
  });
});

</script> 
     </div>
